I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[Feature]: Expose ask_user_questions through the packaged MCP server
## Summary
Expose ask_user_questions through @gsd-build/mcp-server so workflow MCP clients like Claude Code CLI can use structured user questions instead of failing compatibility checks.

## Problem to solve
The packaged MCP server already exposes the headless-safe workflow surface, but it still blocks guided flows that require ask_user_questions. That leaves the Claude Code CLI workflow transport unable to run interactive GSD units even when the client supports MCP elicitation. In local checkout flows, the spawned workflow server could also drift behind source changes because the transport preferred stale dist artifacts.

## Proposed solution
Add an MCP form-elicitation bridge for ask_user_questions in the packaged server, preserve the existing GSD answer JSON shape expected by prompts and write gates, add the tool to the workflow MCP compatibility surface, and make local workflow launches prefer live source modules and source CLI entrypoints when the TS resolve hook is available.

## Alternatives considered
Keeping ask_user_questions unavailable preserves a headless-only package surface, but that continues to block guided workflow units for elicitation-capable clients. Falling back to plain text prompts would bypass the structured answer contract GSD already depends on. Using form elicitation for secure_env_collect was also considered, but that would be the wrong security model for secrets.

## Use cases
- Running guided GSD milestone or slice discussions from Claude Code CLI over workflow MCP
- Allowing write-gated flows that depend on structured confirmation questions to proceed through the packaged server
- Keeping local checkout testing aligned with source changes instead of stale dist output during MCP workflow development

## Impact
Affected: users running GSD workflow MCP through Claude Code CLI or other elicitation-capable clients
Severity: medium
Frequency: whenever a guided workflow unit requires structured user input
Consequence: guided units fail capability checks or cannot collect the structured responses GSD expects

## Evidence or prior art
The in-process GSD extension already exposes ask_user_questions and existing prompts/write-gate logic expect its current JSON answer shape. The MCP SDK supports form elicitation, which is the appropriate transport for non-secret structured choices.

## Additional information
This change should keep secure_env_collect out of scope. That path should use MCP URL elicitation or another secure bridge rather than form elicitation.

</pr_description>

On Unix: /bin/bash, then bash on PATH, then fallback to sh\n */\nexport function getShellConfig(): { shell: string; args: string[] } {\n\tif (cachedShellConfig) {\n\t\treturn cachedShellConfig;\n\t}\n\n\tconst settings = SettingsManager.create();\n\tconst customShellPath = settings.getShellPath();\n\n\t// 1. Control characters (except tab, newline, carriage return)\n * - Lone surrogates\n * - Unicode Format characters (crash string-width due to a bug)\n * - Characters with undefined code points\n */\nexport function sanitizeBinaryOutput(str: string): string {\n\t// Use Array.from to properly iterate over code points (not code units)\n\t// This handles surrogate pairs correctly and catches edge cases where\n\t// codePointAt() might return undefined\n\treturn Array.from(str)\n\t\t.filter((char) => {\n\t\t\t// Filter out characters that cause string-width to crash\n\t\t\t// This includes:\n\t\t\t// - Unicode format characters\n\t\t\t// - Lone surrogates (already filtered by Array.from)\n\t\t\t// - Control chars except \\t \\n \\r\n\t\t\t// - Characters with undefined code points\n\n\t\t\tconst code = char.codePointAt(0);\n\n\t\t\t// Skip if code point is undefined (edge case with invalid strings)\n\t\t\tif (code === undefined) return false;\n\n\t\t\t// Allow tab, newline, carriage return\n\t\t\tif (code === 0x09 || code === 0x0a || code === 0x0d) return true;\n\n\t\t\t// Filter out control characters (0x00-0x1F, except 0x09, 0x0a, 0x0x0d)\n\t\t\tif (code <= 0x1f) return false;\n\n\t\t\t// Filter out Unicode format characters\n\t\t\tif (code >= 0xfff9 && code <= 0xfffb) return false;\n\n\t\t\treturn true;\n\t\t})\n\t\t.join(\"\");\n}\n\n/**\n * Kill a process and all its children (cross-platform)\n */\nexport function killProcessTree(pid: number): void {\n\tif (process.platform === \"win32\") {\n\t\t// Use taskkill on Windows to kill process tree\n\t\ttry {\n\t\t\tspawn(\"taskkill\", [\"/F\", \"/T\", \"/PID\", String(pid)], {\n\t\t\t\tstdio: \"ignore\",\n\t\t\t});\n\t\t} catch {\n\t\t\t// Ignore errors if taskkill fails\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\t// Use SIGKILL on Unix/Linux/Mac\n\t\ttry {\n\t\t\tprocess.kill(-pid, \"SIGKILL\");\n\t\t} catch {\n\t\t\t// Fallback to killing just the child if process group kill fails\n\t\t\ttry {\n\t\t\t\tprocess.kill(pid, \"SIGKILL\");\n\t\t\t} catch {\n\t\t\t\t// Process already dead\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n"]}

as any).pipe(fileStream));\n}\n\nfunction findBinaryRecursively(rootDir: string, binaryFileName: string): string | null {\n\tconst stack: string[] = [rootDir];\n\n\twhile (stack.length > 0) {\n\t\tconst currentDir = stack.pop();\n\t\tif (!currentDir) continue;\n\n\t\tconst entries = readdirSync(currentDir, { withFileTypes: true });\n\t\tfor (const entry of entries) {\n\t\t\tconst getLatestVersion(config.repo);\n\n\t// Get asset name for this platform\n\tconst assetName = config.getAssetName(version, plat, architecture);\n\tif (!assetName) {\n\t\tthrow new Error(`Unsupported platform: ${plat}/${architecture}`);\n\t}\n\n\t// Create tools directory\n\tmkdirSync(TOOLS_DIR, { recursive: true });\n\n\tconst downloadUrl = : \"\";\n\tconst binaryPath = join(TOOLS_DIR, config.binaryName + binaryExt);\n\n\t// Download\n\tawait downloadFile(downloadUrl, archivePath);\n\n\t// Extract into a unique temp directory. fd and rg downloads can run concurrently\n\t// during startup, so sharing a fixed directory causes races.\n\tconst extractDir = join(\n\t\tTOOLS_DIR,\n\t\t`extract_tmp_${config.binaryName}_${process.pid}_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10)}`,\n\t);\n\tmkdirSync(extractDir, { recursive: true });\n\n\ttry extractResult.status !== 0) {\n\t\t\t\tconst errMsg = extractResult.error?.message ?? extractResult.stderr?.toString().trim() ?? \"unknown error\";\n\t\t\t\tthrow new Error(`Failed to extract ${assetName}: ${errMsg}`);\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if (assetName.endsWith(\".zip\")) {\n\t\t\tawait extractZip(archivePath, { dir: extractDir });\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tthrow new Error(`Unsupported archive Offline mode enabled, skipping download.`));\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn undefined;\n\t}\n\n\t// On Android/Termux, Linux binaries don't work due to Bionic libc incompatibility.\n\t// Users must install via pkg.\n\tif (platform() === \"android\") {\n\t\tconst pkgName = TERMUX_PACKAGES[tool] ?? tool;\n\t\tif (!silent) {\n\t\t\tconsole.log(chalk.yellow(`${config.name} not found. Install with: pkg install ${pkgName}`));\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn undefined;\n\t}\n\n\t// Tool not found - download it\n\tif (!silent) {\n\t\tconsole.log(chalk.dim(`${config.name} not found. Downloading...`));\n\t}\n\n\ttry {\n\t\tconst path = await downloadTool(tool);\n\t\tif (!silent) {\n\t\t\tconsole.log(chalk.dim(`${config.name} installed to ${path}`));\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn path;\n\t} catch (e) {\n\t\tif (!silent) {\n\t\t\tconsole.log(chalk.yellow(`Failed to download ${config.name}: ${e instanceof Error ? e.message : e}`));\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn undefined;\n\t}\n}\n"]}

* Resolve configuration values that may be shell commands, environment variables, or literals.\n * Used by auth-storage.ts and model-registry.ts.\n */\n\nimport { execFileSync } from \"child_process\";\nimport { COMMAND_EXECUTION_TIMEOUT_MS } from \"./constants.js\";\n\nconst SHELL_OPERATORS = /[;|&`$><]/;\n\n// Cache for shell command results (persists for process [\n\t\"pass\",\n\t\"op\",\n\t\"aws\",\n\t\"gcloud\",\n\t\"vault\",\n\t\"security\",\n\t\"gpg\",\n\t\"bw\",\n\t\"gopass\",\n\t\"lpass\",\n];\n\n/**\n * Active command prefix allowlist.     30	const SERVER_NAME = 'gsd';
    31	const SERVER_VERSION = '2.53.0';
    32	
    33	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    34	// Tool result helpers
    35	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    36	
    37	/** Wrap a JSON-serializable value as MCP tool content. */
    38	function jsonContent(data: unknown): { content: Array<{ type: 'text'; text: string }> } {
    39	  return { content: [{ type: 'text' as const, text: JSON.stringify(data, null, 2) }] };
    40	}
    41	
    42	/** Return an MCP error response. */
    43	function errorContent(message: string): { isError: true; content: Array<{ type: 'text'; text: string }> } {
    44	  return { isError: true, content: [{ type: 'text' as const, text: message }] };
    45	}
    46	
    47	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    48	// gsd_query filesystem reader
    49	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    50	
    51	async function readProjectState(projectDir: string, _query: string): Promise<Record<string, unknown>> {
    52	  const gsdDir = join(resolve(projectDir), '.gsd');
    53	  const result: Record<string, unknown> = { projectDir: resolve(projectDir) };
    54	
    55	  // STATE.md — current execution state
    56	  try {
    57	    result.state = await readFile(join(gsdDir, 'STATE.md'), 'utf-8');
    58	  } catch {
    59	    result.state = null;
    60	  }
    61	
    62	  // PROJECT.md — project description
    63	  try {
    64	    result.project = await readFile(join(gsdDir, 'PROJECT.md'), 'utf-8');
    65	  } catch {
    66	    result.project = null;
    67	  }
    68	
    69	  // REQUIREMENTS.md — requirement contract
    70	  try {
    71	    result.requirements = await readFile(join(gsdDir, 'REQUIREMENTS.md'), 'utf-8');
    72	  } catch {
    73	    result.requirements = null;
    74	  }
    75	
    76	  // List milestones with basic metadata
    77	  const milestonesDir = join(gsdDir, 'milestones');
    78	  try {
    79	    const entries = await readdir(milestonesDir, { withFileTypes: true });
    80	    const milestones: Array<{ id: string; hasRoadmap: boolean; hasSummary: boolean }> = [];
    81	    for (const entry of entries) {
    82	      if (!entry.isDirectory()) continue;
    83	      const mDir = join(milestonesDir, entry.name);
    84	      const hasRoadmap = await fileExists(join(mDir, `${entry.name}-ROADMAP.md`));
    85	      const hasSummary = await fileExists(join(mDir, `${entry.name}-SUMMARY.md`));
    86	      milestones.push({ id: entry.name, hasRoadmap, hasSummary });
    87	    }
    88	    result.milestones = milestones;
    89	  } catch {
    90	    result.milestones = [];
    91	  }
    92	
    93	  return result;
    94	}
    95	
    96	async function fileExists(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
    97	  try {
    98	    await stat(path);
    99	    return true;
   100	  } catch {
   101	    return false;
   102	  }
   103	}
   104	
   105	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   106	// MCP Server type — minimal interface for the dynamically-imported McpServer
   107	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   108	
   109	interface McpServerInstance {
   110	  tool(name: string, description: string, params: Record<string, unknown>, handler: (args: Record<string, unknown>) => Promise<unknown>): unknown;
   111	  connect(transport: unknown): Promise<void>;
   112	  close(): Promise<void>;
   113	}
   114	
   115	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   116	// createMcpServer
   117	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   118	
   119	/**
   120	 * Create and configure an MCP server with session, read-only, and workflow tools.
   121	 *
   122	 * Returns the McpServer instance — call `connect(transport)` to start serving.
   123	 * Uses dynamic imports for the MCP SDK to avoid TS subpath resolution issues.
   124	 */
   125	export async function createMcpServer(sessionManager: SessionManager): Promise<{
   126	  server: McpServerInstance;
   127	}> {
   128	  // Dynamic import — same workaround as src/mcp-server.ts
   129	  const mcpMod = await import(`${MCP_PKG}/server/mcp.js`);
   130	  const McpServer = mcpMod.McpServer;
   131	
   132	  const server: McpServerInstance = new McpServer(
   133	    { name: SERVER_NAME, version: SERVER_VERSION },
   134	    { capabilities: { tools: {} } },
   135	  );
   136	
   137	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   138	  // gsd_execute — start a new GSD auto-mode session
   139	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   140	  server.tool(
   141	    'gsd_execute',
   142	    'Start a GSD auto-mode session for a project directory. Returns a sessionId for tracking.',
   143	    {
   144	      projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   145	      command: z.string().optional().describe('Command to send (default: "/gsd auto")'),
   146	      model: z.string().optional().describe('Model ID override'),
   147	      bare: z.boolean().optional().describe('Run in bare mode (skip user config)'),
   148	    },
   149	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   150	      const { projectDir, command, model, bare } = args as {
   151	        projectDir: string; command?: string; model?: string; bare?: boolean;
   152	      };
   153	      try {
   154	        const sessionId = await sessionManager.startSession(projectDir, { command, model, bare });
   155	        return jsonContent({ sessionId, status: 'started' });
   156	      } catch (err) {
   157	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   158	      }
   159	    },
   160	  );
   161	
   162	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   163	  // gsd_status — poll session status
   164	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   165	  server.tool(
   166	    'gsd_status',
   167	    'Get the current status of a GSD session including progress, recent events, and pending blockers.',
   168	    {
   169	      sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   170	    },
   171	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   172	      const { sessionId } = args as { sessionId: string };
   173	      try {
   174	        const session = sessionManager.getSession(sessionId);
   175	        if (!session) return errorContent(`Session not found: ${sessionId}`);
   176	
   177	        const durationMs = Date.now() - session.startTime;
   178	        const toolCallCount = session.events.filter(
   179	          (e) => (e as Record<string, unknown>).type === 'tool_use' ||
   180	                 (e as Record<string, unknown>).type === 'tool_execution_start'
   181	        ).length;
   182	
   183	        return jsonContent({
   184	          status: session.status,
   185	          progress: {
   186	            eventCount: session.events.length,
   187	            toolCalls: toolCallCount,
   188	          },
   189	          recentEvents: session.events.slice(-10),
   190	          pendingBlocker: session.pendingBlocker
   191	            ? {
   192	                id: session.pendingBlocker.id,
   193	                method: session.pendingBlocker.method,
   194	                message: session.pendingBlocker.message,
   195	              }
   196	            : null,
   197	          cost: session.cost,
   198	          durationMs,
   199	        });
   200	      } catch (err) {
   201	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   202	      }
   203	    },
   204	  );
   205	
   206	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   207	  // gsd_result — get accumulated session result
   208	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   209	  server.tool(
   210	    'gsd_result',
   211	    'Get the result of a GSD session. Returns partial results if the session is still running.',
   212	    {
   213	      sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   214	    },
   215	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   216	      const { sessionId } = args as { sessionId: string };
   217	      try {
   218	        const result = sessionManager.getResult(sessionId);
   219	        return jsonContent(result);
   220	      } catch (err) {
   221	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   222	      }
   223	    },
   224	  );
   225	
   226	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   227	  // gsd_cancel — cancel a running session
   228	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   229	  server.tool(
   230	    'gsd_cancel',
   231	    'Cancel a running GSD session. Aborts the current operation and stops the process.',
   232	    {
   233	      sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   234	    },
   235	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   236	      const { sessionId } = args as { sessionId: string };
   237	      try {
   238	        await sessionManager.cancelSession(sessionId);
   239	        return jsonContent({ cancelled: true });
   240	      } catch (err) {
   241	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   242	      }
   243	    },
   244	  );
   245	
   246	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   247	  // gsd_query — read project state from filesystem (no session needed)
   248	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   249	  server.tool(
   250	    'gsd_query',
   251	    'Query GSD project state from the filesystem. Returns STATE.md, PROJECT.md, requirements, and milestone listing. Does not require an active session.',
   252	    {
   253	      projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   254	      query: z.string().describe('What to query (e.g. "status", "milestones", "requirements")'),
   255	    },
   256	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   257	      const { projectDir, query } = args as { projectDir: string; query: string };
   258	      try {
   259	        const state = await readProjectState(projectDir, query);
   260	        return jsonContent(state);
   261	      } catch (err) {
   262	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   263	      }
   264	    },
   265	  );
   266	
   267	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   268	  // gsd_resolve_blocker — resolve a pending blocker
   269	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   270	  server.tool(
   271	    'gsd_resolve_blocker',
   272	    'Resolve a pending blocker in a GSD session by sending a response to the UI request.',
   273	    {
   274	      sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   275	      response: z.string().describe('Response to send for the pending blocker'),
   276	    },
   277	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   278	      const { sessionId, response } = args as { sessionId: string; response: string };
   279	      try {
   280	        await sessionManager.resolveBlocker(sessionId, response);
   281	        return jsonContent({ resolved: true });
   282	      } catch (err) {
   283	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   284	      }
   285	    },
   286	  );
   287	
   288	  // =======================================================================
   289	  // READ-ONLY TOOLS — no session required, pure filesystem reads
   290	  // =======================================================================
   291	
   292	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   293	  // gsd_progress — structured project progress metrics
   294	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   295	  server.tool(
   296	    'gsd_progress',
   297	    'Get structured project progress: active milestone/slice/task, phase, completion counts, blockers, and next action. No session required — reads directly from .gsd/ on disk.',
   298	    {
   299	      projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   300	    },
   301	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   302	      const { projectDir } = args as { projectDir: string };
   303	      try {
   304	        return jsonContent(readProgress(projectDir));
   305	      } catch (err) {
   306	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   307	      }
   308	    },
   309	  );
   310	
   311	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   312	  // gsd_roadmap — milestone/slice/task structure with status
   313	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   314	  server.tool(
   315	    'gsd_roadmap',
   316	    'Get the full project roadmap structure: milestones with their slices, tasks, status, risk, and dependencies. Optionally filter to a single milestone. No session required.',
   317	    {
   318	      projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   319	      milestoneId: z.string().optional().describe('Filter to a specific milestone (e.g. "M001")'),
   320	    },
   321	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   322	      const { projectDir, milestoneId } = args as { projectDir: string; milestoneId?: string };
   323	      try {
   324	        return jsonContent(readRoadmap(projectDir, milestoneId));
   325	      } catch (err) {
   326	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   327	      }
   328	    },
   329	  );
   330	
   331	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   332	  // gsd_history — execution history with cost/token metrics
   333	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   334	  server.tool(
   335	    'gsd_history',
   336	    'Get execution history with cost, token usage, model, and duration per unit. Returns totals across all units. No session required.',
   337	    {
   338	      projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   339	      limit: z.number().optional().describe('Max entries to return (most recent first). Default: all.'),
   340	    },
   341	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   342	      const { projectDir, limit } = args as { projectDir: string; limit?: number };
   343	      try {
   344	        return jsonContent(readHistory(projectDir, limit));
   345	      } catch (err) {
   346	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   347	      }
   348	    },
   349	  );
   350	
   351	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   352	  // gsd_doctor — lightweight structural health check
   353	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   354	  server.tool(
   355	    'gsd_doctor',
   356	    'Run a lightweight structural health check on the .gsd/ directory. Checks for missing files, status inconsistencies, and orphaned state. No session required.',
   357	    {
   358	      projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   359	      scope: z.string().optional().describe('Limit checks to a specific milestone (e.g. "M001")'),
   360	    },
   361	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   362	      const { projectDir, scope } = args as { projectDir: string; scope?: string };
   363	      try {
   364	        return jsonContent(runDoctorLite(projectDir, scope));
   365	      } catch (err) {
   366	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   367	      }
   368	    },
   369	  );
   370

   380	    },

   251	function getAllowedProjectRoot(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env): string | null {
   252	  const configuredRoot = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim();
   253	  return configuredRoot ? resolve(configuredRoot) : null;
   254	}
   255	
   256	function isWithinRoot(candidatePath: string, rootPath: string): boolean {
   257	  const rel = relative(rootPath, candidatePath);
   258	  return rel === "" || (!rel.startsWith("..") && !isAbsolute(rel));
   259	}
   260	
   261	function validateProjectDir(projectDir: string, env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env): string {
   262	  if (!isAbsolute(projectDir)) {
   263	    throw new Error(`projectDir must be an absolute path. Received: ${projectDir}`);
   264	  }
   265	
   266	  const resolvedProjectDir = resolve(projectDir);
   267	  const allowedRoot = getAllowedProjectRoot(env);
   268	  if (allowedRoot && !isWithinRoot(resolvedProjectDir, allowedRoot)) {
   269	    throw new Error(
   270	      `projectDir must stay within the configured workflow project root. Received: ${resolvedProjectDir}; allowed root: ${allowedRoot}`,
   271	    );
   272	  }
   273	
   274	  return resolvedProjectDir;
   275	}

   277	function parseToolArgs<T>(schema: z.ZodType<T>, args: Record<string, unknown>): T {
   278	  return schema.parse(args);
   279	}
   280	
   281	function parseWorkflowArgs<T extends { projectDir: string }>(
   282	  schema: z.ZodType<T>,
   283	  args: Record<string, unknown>,
   284	): T {
   285	  const parsed = parseToolArgs(schema, args);
   286	  return {
   287	    ...parsed,
   288	    projectDir: validateProjectDir(parsed.projectDir),
   289	  };
   290	}

   292	function isWorkflowToolExecutors(value: unknown): value is WorkflowToolExecutors {
   293	  if (!value || typeof value !== "object") return false;
   294	  const record = value as Record<string, unknown>;
   295	  const functionExports = [

   310	    functionExports.every((key) => typeof record[key] === "function");

   317	function getWriteGateModuleCandidates(): string[] {
   318	  const candidates: string[] = [];
   319	  const explicitModule = process.env.GSD_WORKFLOW_WRITE_GATE_MODULE?.trim();
   320	  if (explicitModule) {
   321	    if (/^[a-z]{2,}:/i.test(explicitModule) && !explicitModule.startsWith("file:")) {
   322	      throw new Error("GSD_WORKFLOW_WRITE_GATE_MODULE only supports file: URLs or filesystem paths.");
   323	    }
   324	    candidates.push(explicitModule.startsWith("file:") ? explicitModule : toFileUrl(explicitModule));
   325	  }
   326	
   327	  candidates.push(
   328	    new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/bootstrap/write-gate.js", import.meta.url).href,
   329	    new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/bootstrap/write-gate.ts", import.meta.url).href,
   330	  );
   331	
   332	  return [...new Set(candidates)];
   333	}

   339	function getWorkflowExecutorModuleCandidates(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env): string[] {
   340	  const candidates: string[] = [];
   341	  const explicitModule = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE?.trim();
   342	  if (explicitModule) {
   343	    if (/^[a-z]{2,}:/i.test(explicitModule) && !explicitModule.startsWith("file:")) {
   344	      throw new Error("GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE only supports file: URLs or filesystem paths.");
   345	    }
   346	    candidates.push(explicitModule.startsWith("file:") ? explicitModule : toFileUrl(explicitModule));
   347	  }
   348	
   349	  candidates.push(
   350	    new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.js", import.meta.url).href,
   351	    new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.ts", import.meta.url).href,
   352	  );
   353

   357	async function getWorkflowToolExecutors(): Promise<WorkflowToolExecutors> {
   358	  if (!workflowToolExecutorsPromise) {
   359	    workflowToolExecutorsPromise = (async () => {
   360	      const attempts: string[] = [];
   361	      for (const candidate of getWorkflowExecutorModuleCandidates()) {
   362	        try {
   363	          const loaded = await import(candidate);
   364	          if (isWorkflowToolExecutors(loaded)) {
   365	            return loaded;
   366	          }
   367	          attempts.push(`${candidate} (module shape mismatch)`);
   368	        } catch (err) {
   369	          attempts.push(`${candidate} (${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)})`);
   370	        }
   371	      }
   372	
   373	      throw new Error(
   374	        "Unable to load GSD workflow executor bridge for MCP mutation tools. " +
   375	        "Set GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE to an importable workflow-tool-executors module, " +
   376	        "or run the MCP server from a GSD checkout that includes src/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.(js|ts). " +
   377	        `Attempts: ${attempts.join("; ")}`,
   378	      );
   379	    })();
   380	  }
   381	  return workflowToolExecutorsPromise;
   382	}
   383	
   384	async function getWorkflowWriteGateModule(): Promise<WorkflowWriteGateModule> {
   385	  if (!workflowWriteGatePromise) {
   386	    workflowWriteGatePromise = (async () => {
   387	      const attempts: string[] = [];
   388	      for (const candidate of getWriteGateModuleCandidates()) {
   389	        try {
   390	          const loaded = await import(candidate);
   391	          if (
   392	            loaded &&
   393	            typeof loaded.loadWriteGateSnapshot === "function" &&
   394	            typeof loaded.shouldBlockPendingGateInSnapshot === "function" &&
   395	            typeof loaded.shouldBlockQueueExecutionInSnapshot === "function"
   396	          ) {
   397	            return loaded as WorkflowWriteGateModule;
   398	          }
   399	          attempts.push(`${candidate} (module shape mismatch)`);
   400	        } catch (err) {
   401	          attempts.push(`${candidate} (${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)})`);
   402	        }
   403	      }
   404	
   405	      throw new Error(
   406	        "Unable to load GSD write-gate bridge for workflow MCP tools. " +
   407	        `Attempts: ${attempts.join("; ")}`,
   408	      );
   409	    })();
   410	  }
   411	  return workflowWriteGatePromise;
   412	}

   414	interface McpToolServer {
   415	  tool(
   416	    name: string,
   417	    description: string,
   418	    params: Record<string, unknown>,
   419	    handler: (args: Record<string, unknown>) => Promise<unknown>,
   420	  ): unknown;
   421	}
   422	
   423	async function runSerializedWorkflowOperation<T>(fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
   424	  // The shared DB adapter and workflow log base path are process-global, so
   425	  // workflow MCP mutations must not overlap within a single server process.
   426	  const prior = workflowExecutionQueue;
   427	  let release!: () => void;
   428	  workflowExecutionQueue = new Promise<void>((resolve) => {
   429	    release = resolve;
   430	  });
   431	
   432	  await prior;
   433	  try {
   434	    return await fn();
   435	  } finally {
   436	    release();
   437	  }
   438	}
   439	
   440	async function enforceWorkflowWriteGate(
   441	  toolName: string,
   442	  projectDir: string,
   443	  milestoneId: string | null = null,
   444	): Promise<void> {
   445	  const writeGate = await getWorkflowWriteGateModule();
   446	  const snapshot = writeGate.loadWriteGateSnapshot(projectDir);
   447	  const pendingGate = writeGate.shouldBlockPendingGateInSnapshot(
   448	    snapshot,
   449	    toolName,
   450	    milestoneId,
   451	    snapshot.activeQueuePhase,
   452	  );
   453	  if (pendingGate.block) {
   454	    throw new Error(pendingGate.reason ?? "workflow tool blocked by pending discussion gate");
   455	  }
   456	
   457	  const queueGuard = writeGate.shouldBlockQueueExecutionInSnapshot(
   458	    snapshot,
   459	    toolName,
   460	    "",
   461	    snapshot.activeQueuePhase,
   462	  );
   463	  if (queueGuard.block) {
   464	    throw new Error(queueGuard.reason ?? "workflow tool blocked during queue mode");
   465	  }
   466	}

   468	async function handleTaskComplete(
   469	  projectDir: string,
   470	  args: Omit<z.infer<typeof taskCompleteSchema>, "projectDir">,
   471	): Promise<unknown> {
   472	  await enforceWorkflowWriteGate("gsd_task_complete", projectDir, args.milestoneId);
   473	  const {
   474	    taskId,
   475	    sliceId,
   476	    milestoneId,
   477	    oneLiner,
   478	    narrative,
   479	    verification,
   480	    deviations,
   481	    knownIssues,
   482	    keyFiles,
   483	    keyDecisions,
   484	    blockerDiscovered,
   485	    verificationEvidence,
   486	  } = args;
   487	  const { executeTaskComplete } = await getWorkflowToolExecutors();
   488	  return runSerializedWorkflowOperation(() =>
   489	    executeTaskComplete(
   490	      {
   491	        taskId,
   492	        sliceId,
   493	        milestoneId,
   494	        oneLiner,
   495	        narrative,
   496	        verification,
   497	        deviations,
   498	        knownIssues,
   499	        keyFiles,
   500	        keyDecisions,
   501	        blockerDiscovered,
   502	        verificationEvidence,
   503	      },
   504	      projectDir,
   505	    ),
   506	  );
   507	}

   509	async function handleSliceComplete(
   510	  projectDir: string,
   511	  args: z.infer<typeof sliceCompleteSchema>,
   512	): Promise<unknown> {
   513	  await enforceWorkflowWriteGate("gsd_slice_complete", projectDir, args.milestoneId);
   514	  const { executeSliceComplete } = await getWorkflowToolExecutors();
   515	  const { projectDir: _projectDir, ...params } = args;
   516	  return runSerializedWorkflowOperation(() => executeSliceComplete(params, projectDir));

    43	function parseLookupOutput(output: Buffer | string): string {
    44	  return output
    45	    .toString()
    46	    .trim()
    47	    .split(/\r?\n/)[0] ?? "";
    48	}
    49	
    50	function parseJsonEnv<T>(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv, name: string): T | undefined {
    51	  const raw = env[name];
    52	  if (!raw) return undefined;
    53	  try {
    54	    return JSON.parse(raw) as T;
    55	  } catch {
    56	    throw new Error(`Invalid JSON in ${name}`);
    57	  }
    58	}
    59	
    60	function lookupCommand(command: string, platform: NodeJS.Platform = process.platform): string | null {
    61	  const lookup = platform === "win32" ? `where ${command}` : `which ${command}`;
    62	  try {
    63	    const resolved = parseLookupOutput(execSync(lookup, { timeout: 5_000, stdio: "pipe" }));
    64	    return resolved || null;
    65	  } catch {
    66	    return null;
    67	  }
    68	}
    69	
    70	function findWorkflowCliFromAncestorPath(startPath: string): string | null {
    71	  let current = resolve(startPath);
    72	
    73	  while (true) {
    74	    const candidate = resolve(current, "packages", "mcp-server", "dist", "cli.js");
    75	    if (existsSync(candidate)) return candidate;
    76	
    77	    const parent = dirname(current);
    78	    if (parent === current) break;
    79	    current = parent;
    80	  }
    81	
    82	  return null;
    83	}
    84	
    85	function getBundledWorkflowMcpCliPath(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv): string | null {
    86	  const envAnchors = [
    87	    env.GSD_BIN_PATH?.trim(),
    88	    env.GSD_CLI_PATH?.trim(),
    89	    env.GSD_WORKFLOW_PATH?.trim(),
    90	  ].filter((value): value is string => typeof value === "string" && value.length > 0);
    91	
    92	  for (const anchor of envAnchors) {
    93	    const candidate = findWorkflowCliFromAncestorPath(anchor);
    94	    if (candidate) return candidate;
    95	  }
    96	
    97	  const candidates = [
    98	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../packages/mcp-server/dist/cli.js", import.meta.url))),
    99	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../../packages/mcp-server/dist/cli.js", import.meta.url))),
   100	  ];
   101	
   102	  for (const bundledCli of candidates) {
   103	    if (existsSync(bundledCli)) return bundledCli;
   104	  }
   105	
   106	  return null;
   107	}

   123	function getBundledWorkflowWriteGateModulePath(): string | null {
   124	  const candidates = [
   125	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../dist/resources/extensions/gsd/bootstrap/write-gate.js", import.meta.url))),
   126	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("./bootstrap/write-gate.js", import.meta.url))),
   127	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("./bootstrap/write-gate.ts", import.meta.url))),
   128	  ];
   129	
   130	  for (const candidate of candidates) {
   131	    if (existsSync(candidate)) return candidate;
   132	  }
   133	
   134	  return null;
   135	}
   136	
   137	function buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(
   138	  projectRoot: string,
   139	  gsdCliPath: string | undefined,
   140	  explicitEnv?: Record<string, string>,
   141	): Record<string, string> {
   142	  const executorModulePath = getBundledWorkflowExecutorModulePath();
   143	  const writeGateModulePath = getBundledWorkflowWriteGateModulePath();
   144	
   145	  return {
   146	    ...(explicitEnv ?? {}),
   147	    ...(gsdCliPath ? { GSD_CLI_PATH: gsdCliPath } : {}),
   148	    ...(executorModulePath ? { GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE: executorModulePath } : {}),
   149	    ...(writeGateModulePath ? { GSD_WORKFLOW_WRITE_GATE_MODULE: writeGateModulePath } : {}),
   150	    GSD_PERSIST_WRITE_GATE_STATE: "1",
   151	    GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT: projectRoot,
   152	  };
   153	}
   154	
   155	export function detectWorkflowMcpLaunchConfig(
   156	  projectRoot = process.cwd(),
   157	  env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env,
   158	): WorkflowMcpLaunchConfig | null {
   159	  const name = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_NAME?.trim() || "gsd-workflow";
   160	  const explicitCommand = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_COMMAND?.trim();
   161	  const explicitArgs = parseJsonEnv<unknown>(env, "GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_ARGS");
   162	  const explicitEnv = parseJsonEnv<Record<string, string>>(env, "GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_ENV");
   163	  const explicitCwd = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_CWD?.trim();
   164	  const gsdCliPath = env.GSD_CLI_PATH?.trim() || env.GSD_BIN_PATH?.trim();
   165	  const workflowProjectRoot =
   166	    explicitEnv?.GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim() ||
   167	    env.GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim() ||
   168	    env.GSD_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim() ||
   169	    explicitCwd ||
   170	    projectRoot;
   171	  const resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot = resolve(workflowProjectRoot);
   172	
   173	  if (explicitCommand) {
   174	    const launchEnv = buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolve(workflowProjectRoot), gsdCliPath, explicitEnv);
   175	    return {
   176	      name,
   177	      command: explicitCommand,
   178	      args: Array.isArray(explicitArgs) && explicitArgs.length > 0 ? explicitArgs.map(String) : undefined,
   179	      cwd: explicitCwd || undefined,
   180	      env: Object.keys(launchEnv).length > 0 ? launchEnv : undefined,
   181	    };
   182	  }
   183	
   184	  const distCli = resolve(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, "packages", "mcp-server", "dist", "cli.js");
   185	  if (existsSync(distCli)) {
   186	    return {
   187	      name,
   188	      command: process.execPath,
   189	      args: [distCli],
   190	      cwd: resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot,
   191	      env: buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, gsdCliPath),
   192	    };
   193	  }
   194	
   195	  const bundledCli = getBundledWorkflowMcpCliPath(env);
   196	  if (bundledCli) {
   197	    return {
   198	      name,
   199	      command: process.execPath,
   200	      args: [bundledCli],
   201	      cwd: resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot,
   202	      env: buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, gsdCliPath),
   203	    };
   204	  }
   205	
   206	  const binPath = lookupCommand("gsd-mcp-server");
   207	  if (binPath) {
   208	    return {
   209	      name,
   210	      command: binPath,
   211	      env: buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, gsdCliPath),
   212	    };
   213	  }
   214	
   215	  return null;
   216	}
   217	
   218	export function buildWorkflowMcpServers(
   219	  projectRoot = process.cwd(),
   220	  env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env,
   221	): Record<string, Record<string, unknown>> | undefined {
   222	  const launch = detectWorkflowMcpLaunchConfig(projectRoot, env);
   223	  if (!launch) return undefined;
   224	
   225	  return {
   226	    [launch.name]: {
   227	      command: launch.command,
   228	      ...(launch.args && launch.args.length > 0 ? { args: launch.args } : {}),
   229	      ...(launch.env ? { env: launch.env } : {}),
   230	      ...(launch.cwd ? { cwd: launch.cwd } : {}),
   231	    },
   232	  };
   233	}
   234	
   235	export function getRequiredWorkflowToolsForGuidedUnit(unitType: string): string[] {
   236	  switch (unitType) {
   237	    case "discuss-milestone":
   238	      return ["gsd_summary_save", "gsd_plan_milestone"];
   239	    case "discuss-slice":
   240	      return ["gsd_summary_save"];
   241	    case "research-milestone":
   242	    case "research-slice":
   243	      return ["gsd_summary_save"];
   244	    case "plan-milestone":
   245	      return ["gsd_plan_milestone"];
   246	    case "plan-slice":
   247	      return ["gsd_plan_slice"];
   248	    case "execute-task":
   249	      return ["gsd_task_complete"];
   250	    case "complete-slice":
   251	      return ["gsd_slice_complete"];
   252	    default:
   253	      return [];
   254	  }
   255	}
   256	
   257	export function getRequiredWorkflowToolsForAutoUnit(unitType: string): string[] {
   258	  switch (unitType) {
   259	    case "discuss-milestone":
   260	      return ["gsd_summary_save", "gsd_plan_milestone"];
   261	    case "research-milestone":
   262	    case "research-slice":
   263	    case "run-uat":
   264	      return ["gsd_summary_save"];
   265	    case "plan-milestone":
   266	      return ["gsd_plan_milestone"];
   267	    case "plan-slice":
   268	      return ["gsd_plan_slice"];
   269	    case "execute-task":
   270	    case "execute-task-simple":
   271	    case "reactive-execute":
   272	      return ["gsd_complete_task"];
   273	    case "complete-slice":
   274	      return ["gsd_complete_slice"];
   275	    case "replan-slice":
   276	      return ["gsd_replan_slice"];
   277	    case "reassess-roadmap":
   278	      return ["gsd_milestone_status", "gsd_reassess_roadmap"];
   279	    case "gate-evaluate":
   280	      return ["gsd_save_gate_result"];
   281	    case "validate-milestone":
   282	      return ["gsd_milestone_status", "gsd_validate_milestone"];
   283	    case "complete-milestone":
   284	      return ["gsd_milestone_status", "gsd_complete_milestone"];
   285	    default:
   286	      return [];
   287	  }
   288	}
   289	
   290	export function usesWorkflowMcpTransport(
   291	  authMode: WorkflowCapabilityOptions["authMode"],
   292	  baseUrl: string | undefined,
   293	): boolean {
   294	  return authMode === "externalCli" && typeof baseUrl === "string" && baseUrl.startsWith("local://");
   295	}
   296	
   297	export function getWorkflowTransportSupportError(
   298	  provider: string | undefined,
   299	  requiredTools: string[],
   300	  options: WorkflowCapabilityOptions = {},
   301	): string | null {
   302	  if (!provider || requiredTools.length === 0) return null;
   303	  if (!usesWorkflowMcpTransport(options.authMode, options.baseUrl)) return null;
   304	
   305	  const projectRoot = options.projectRoot ?? process.cwd();
   306	  const env = options.env ?? process.env;
   307	  const launch = detectWorkflowMcpLaunchConfig(projectRoot, env);
   308	  const surface = options.surface ?? "workflow dispatch";
   309	  const unitLabel = options.unitType ? ` for ${options.unitType}` : "";
   310	  const providerLabel = `"${provider}"`;
   311	
   312	  if (!launch) {
   313	    return `Provider ${providerLabel} cannot run ${surface}${unitLabel}: the GSD workflow MCP server is not configured or discoverable. Configure GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_COMMAND, build packages/mcp-server/dist/cli.js, or install gsd-mcp-server on PATH.`;
   314	  }
   315	
   316	  const missing = [...new Set(requiredTools)].filter((tool) => !MCP_WORKFLOW_TOOL_SURFACE.has(tool));
   317	  if (missing.length === 0) return null;
   318	
   319	  return `Provider ${providerLabel} cannot run ${surface}${unitLabel}: this unit requires ${missing.join(", ")}, but the workflow MCP transport currently exposes only ${Array.from(MCP_WORKFLOW_TOOL_SURFACE).sort().join(", ")}.`;
   320	}

/**
 * High-level MCP server that provides a simpler API for working with resources, tools, and prompts.
 * For advanced usage (like sending notifications or setting custom request handlers), use the underlying
 * Server instance available via the `server` property.
 */

/**
 * The client's response to an elicitation/create request from the server.
 */
export const ElicitResultSchema = ResultSchema.extend({
    /**
     * The user action in response to the elicitation.
     * - "accept": User submitted the form/confirmed the action
     * - "decline": User explicitly decline the action
     * - "cancel": User dismissed without making an explicit choice
     */
    action: z.enum(['accept', 'decline', 'cancel']),
    /**
     * The submitted form data, only present when action is "accept".
     * Contains values matching the requested schema.
     * Per MCP spec, content is "typically omitted" for decline/cancel actions.
     * We normalize null to undefined for leniency while maintaining type compatibility.
     */
    content: z.preprocess(val => (val === null ? undefined : val), z.record(z.string(), z.union([z.string(), z.number(), z.boolean(), z.array(z.string())])).optional())
});

     2	 * Request User Input — LLM tool for asking the user questions
     3	 *
     4	 * Thin wrapper around the shared interview-ui. The LLM presents 1-3
     5	 * questions with 2-3 options each. Each question can be single-select (default)
     6	 * or multi-select (allowMultiple: true). A free-form "None of the above" option
     7	 * is added automatically to single-select questions.
     8	 *
     9	 * Based on: https://github.com/openai/codex (codex-rs/core/src/tools/handlers/ask_user_questions.rs)
    10	 */

    74	
    75	// ─── Per-turn deduplication ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    76	// Prevents duplicate question dispatches (especially to remote channels like
    77	// Discord) when the LLM calls ask_user_questions multiple times with the same
    78	// questions in a single turn. Keyed by full canonicalized payload (id, header,
    79	// question, options, allowMultiple) — not just IDs — so that calls with the
    80	// same IDs but different text/options are treated as distinct.
    81	
    82	import { createHash } from "node:crypto";
    83	
    84	interface CachedResult {
    85	        content: { type: "text"; text: string }[];
    86	        details: AskUserQuestionsDetails;
    87	}
    88	
    89	const turnCache = new Map<string, CachedResult>();
    90	
    91	/** @internal Exported for testing only. */
    92	export function questionSignature(questions: Question[]): string {
    93	        const canonical = questions
    94	                .map((q) => ({
    95	                        id: q.id,
    96	                        header: q.header,
    97	                        question: q.question,
    98	                        options: (q.options || []).map((o) => ({ label: o.label, description: o.description })),
    99	                        allowMultiple: !!q.allowMultiple,
   100	                }))
   101	                .sort((a, b) => a.id.localeCompare(b.id));
   102	        return createHash("sha256").update(JSON.stringify(canonical)).digest("hex").slice(0, 16);
   103	}
   104	
   105	/** Reset the dedup cache. Called on session boundaries. */
   106	export function resetAskUserQuestionsCache(): void {
   107	        turnCache.clear();
   108	}
   109	
   110	// ─── Race helper ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   111	
   112	interface RaceableResult {
   113	        content: { type: "text"; text: string }[];
   114	        details?: unknown;
   115	}
   116	
   117	/**
   118	 * Race a remote channel dispatch against the local TUI. The first to produce
   119	 * a valid (non-error, non-timeout) result wins. The loser is cancelled via
   120	 * the shared AbortController.
   121	 *
   122	 * If the local TUI responds first, the remote poll is aborted (the message
   123	 * stays in Discord/Slack but polling stops). If remote responds first, the
   124	 * local TUI prompt is cancelled.
   125	 *
   126	 * Returns null only when both sides fail or are cancelled.
   127	 */
   128	async function raceRemoteAndLocal(
   129	        startRemote: () => Promise<RaceableResult | null>,
   130	        startLocal: () => Promise<RoundResult | null | undefined>,
   131	        controller: AbortController,
   132	        questions: Question[],
   133	): Promise<RaceableResult | null> {
   134	        // Wrap local TUI result into the same shape as remote results
   135	        const localPromise = startLocal().then((result): RaceableResult | null => {
   136	                if (!result || Object.keys(result.answers).length === 0) return null;
   137	                return {
   138	                        content: [{ type: "text" as const, text: formatForLLM(result) }],
   139	                        details: { questions, response: result, cancelled: false } satisfies LocalResultDetails,
   140	                };
   141	        }).catch(() => null);
   142	
   143	        const remotePromise = startRemote().then((result): RaceableResult | null => {
   144	                if (!result) return null;
   145	                const details = result.details as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
   146	                // Treat timeouts and errors as non-wins — let the local TUI win instead
   147	                if (details?.timed_out || details?.error) return null;
   148	                return result;
   149	        }).catch(() => null);
   150	
   151	        // Race: first non-null result wins
   152	        const winner = await Promise.race([
   153	                localPromise.then((r) => r ? { source: "local" as const, result: r } : null),
   154	                remotePromise.then((r) => r ? { source: "remote" as const, result: r } : null),
   155	        ]);
   156	
   157	        if (winner) {
   158	                // Cancel the loser
   159	                controller.abort();
   160	                return winner.result;
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        // First to resolve was null — wait for the other
   164	        const [localResult, remoteResult] = await Promise.all([localPromise, remotePromise]);
   165	        controller.abort();
   166	        return localResult ?? remoteResult;
   167	}
   168	
   169	// ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   170	
   171	const OTHER_OPTION_LABEL = "None of the above";
   172	
   173	function errorResult(
   174	        message: string,
   175	        questions: Question[] = [],
   176	): { content: { type: "text"; text: string }[]; details: AskUserQuestionsDetails } {
   177	        return {
   178	                content: [{ type: "text", text: sanitizeError(message) }],
   179	                details: { questions, response: null, cancelled: true },
   180	        };
   181	}
   182	
   183	/** Convert the shared RoundResult into the JSON the LLM expects. */
   184	function formatForLLM(result: RoundResult): string {
   185	        const answers: Record<string, { answers: string[] }> = {};
   186	        for (const [id, answer] of Object.entries(result.answers)) {
   187	                const list: string[] = [];
   188	                if (Array.isArray(answer.selected)) {
   189	                        list.push(...answer.selected);
   190	                } else {
   191	                        list.push(answer.selected);
   192	                }
   193	                if (answer.notes) {
   194	                        list.push(`user_note: ${answer.notes}`);
   195	                }
   196	                answers[id] = { answers: list };
   197	        }
   198	        return JSON.stringify({ answers });
   199	}
   200	
   201	// ─── Extension ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

 * dispatching. This ensures guided-flow dispatches respect the same
 * per-phase model preferences that auto-mode uses.
 */
async function dispatchWorkflow(
  pi: ExtensionAPI,
  note: string,
  customType = "gsd-run",
  ctx?: ExtensionContext,
  unitType?: string,
): Promise<void> {
  // Route through the dynamic routing pipeline (complexity classification,
  // tier downgrade, fallback chains) — same path as auto-mode dispatches (#2958).
  if (ctx && unitType) {
    const prefs = loadEffectiveGSDPreferences()?.preferences;
    const result = await selectAndApplyModel(
      ctx, pi, unitType, /* unitId */ "", /* basePath */ process.cwd(),
      prefs, /* verbose */ false, /* autoModeStartModel */ null,
    );
    if (result.appliedModel) {
      debugLog("guided-flow-model-applied", {
        unitType,
        model: `${result.appliedModel.provider}/${result.appliedModel.id}`,
        routing: result.routing,
      });
    }

    const compatibilityError = getWorkflowTransportSupportError(
      result.appliedModel?.provider ?? ctx.model?.provider,
      getRequiredWorkflowToolsForGuidedUnit(unitType),
      {
        projectRoot: process.cwd(),
        surface: "guided flow",
        unitType,
        authMode: result.appliedModel?.provider
          ? ctx.modelRegistry.getProviderAuthMode(result.appliedModel.provider)
          : ctx.model?.provider
            ? ctx.modelRegistry.getProviderAuthMode(ctx.model.provider)
            : undefined,
        baseUrl: result.appliedModel?.baseUrl ?? ctx.model?.baseUrl,
      },
    );
    if (compatibilityError) {
      ctx.ui.notify(compatibilityError, "error");
      return;
    }
  }

  // Scope tools for discuss flows (#2949).
  // Providers with grammar-based constrained decoding (xAI/Grok) return
  // "Grammar is too complex" when the combined tool schema is too large.
  // Discuss flows only need a small subset of GSD tools — strip the heavy

     1	import { existsSync, readFileSync } from 'node:fs';
     2	import { createRequire } from 'node:module';
     3	import { fileURLToPath } from 'node:url';
     4	
     5	const require = createRequire(import.meta.url);
     6	
     7	const ROOT = new URL("../../../../../", import.meta.url);
     8	
     9	export function resolve(specifier, context, nextResolve) {
    10	  // 1. Redirect all workspace package bare imports to source.
    11	  //    CI portability runs don't build any packages/ dist artifacts, so every
    12	  //    @gsd/* specifier (including transitive ones pulled in by pi-coding-agent
    13	  //    source itself) must resolve to the TypeScript source entrypoint.
    14	  if (specifier === "../../packages/pi-coding-agent/src/index.js") {
    15	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-coding-agent/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    16	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/pi-coding-agent") {
    17	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-coding-agent/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    18	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/pi-ai/oauth") {
    19	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-ai/src/utils/oauth/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    20	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/pi-ai") {
    21	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-ai/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    22	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/pi-agent-core") {
    23	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-agent-core/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    24	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/pi-tui") {
    25	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-tui/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    26	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/native") {
    27	    specifier = new URL("packages/native/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    28	  } else if (specifier.startsWith("@gsd/native/")) {
    29	    // Sub-path imports like @gsd/native/fd, @gsd/native/text, etc.
    30	    const subpath = specifier.slice("@gsd/native/".length);
    31	    specifier = new URL(`packages/native/src/${subpath}/index.ts`, ROOT).href;
    32	  }
    33	  // 2. Redirect packages/*/dist/ → packages/*/src/ with .js→.ts for strip-types
    34	  //    Also handles local imports — skip rewrite for dist/ paths that are real compiled artifacts.
    35	
    36	  else if (specifier.endsWith('.js') && (specifier.startsWith('./') || specifier.startsWith('../'))) {
    37	    if (context.parentURL && context.parentURL.includes('/src/')) {
    38	      if (specifier.includes('/dist/')) {
    39	        specifier = specifier.replace('/dist/', '/src/').replace(/\.js$/, '.ts');
    40	      } else {
    41	        specifier = specifier.replace(/\.js$/, '.ts');
    42	      }
    43	    }
    44	  }
    45	  // 3. Extensionless relative imports from web/ (Next.js convention).
    46	  //    Transpiled .tsx files emit extensionless imports — try .ts then .tsx.
    47	  else if (
    48	    (specifier.startsWith('./') || specifier.startsWith('../')) &&
    49	    !specifier.match(/\.\w+$/) &&
    50	    context.parentURL &&
    51	    context.parentURL.includes('/web/')
    52	  ) {
    53	    const baseUrl = new URL(specifier, context.parentURL);
    54	    for (const ext of ['.ts', '.tsx']) {
    55	      const candidate = fileURLToPath(baseUrl) + ext;
    56	      if (existsSync(candidate)) {
    57	        specifier = baseUrl.href + ext;
    58	        break;
    59	      }
    60	
    61	    }
    62	  }
    63	
    64	  return nextResolve(specifier, context);
    65	}
    66	
    67	export function load(url, context, nextLoad) {
    68	  // Node's --experimental-strip-types handles plain .ts but not .tsx and not
    69	  // all TypeScript syntax used by workspace packages (parameter properties,
    70	  // decorators, etc.). Transpile all workspace package source files and .tsx
    71	  // files through TypeScript's transpileModule to avoid those crashes.
    72	  const shouldTranspileWithTypeScript =
    73	    url.endsWith('.tsx') ||
    74	    (url.endsWith('.ts') && url.includes('/packages/') && url.includes('/src/'));
    75	
    76	  if (shouldTranspileWithTypeScript) {
    77	    const ts = require('typescript');
    78	    const source = readFileSync(fileURLToPath(url), 'utf-8');
    79	    const { outputText } = ts.transpileModule(source, {
    80	      fileName: fileURLToPath(url),
    81	      compilerOptions: {
    82	        jsx: ts.JsxEmit.ReactJSX,
    83	        module: ts.ModuleKind.ESNext,
    84	        target: ts.ScriptTarget.ESNext,
    85	        esModuleInterop: true,
    86	        experimentalDecorators: true,
    87	        emitDecoratorMetadata: true,
    88	      },
    89	    });
    90	    // Inject CJS-compatible globals (__dirname, __filename, require) so that
    91	    // workspace packages compiled as ESM can still use them.  This avoids the
    92	    // need for import.meta.url behind indirect invocation patterns that fail in
    93	    // CJS and in dynamically-created scopes.
    94	    // Only inject globals that the source file doesn't already declare itself.
    95	    const preambleLines = [
    96	      'import { fileURLToPath as __preamble_fUTP } from "node:url";',
    97	      'import { dirname as __preamble_dn } from "node:path";',
    98	      'import { createRequire as __preamble_cR } from "node:module";',
    99	    ];
   100	    if (!outputText.includes('const __filename') && !outputText.includes('let __filename')) {
   101	      preambleLines.push('const __filename = __preamble_fUTP(import.meta.url);');
   102	    }
   103	    if (!outputText.includes('const __dirname') && !outputText.includes('let __dirname')) {
   104	      preambleLines.push('const __dirname = __preamble_dn(__preamble_fUTP(import.meta.url));');
   105	    }
   106	    if (!outputText.includes('const require') && !outputText.includes('let require')) {
   107	      preambleLines.push('const require = __preamble_cR(import.meta.url);');
   108	    }
   109	    return { format: 'module', source: preambleLines.join('\n') + '\n' + outputText, shortCircuit: true };
   110	  }
   111	  return nextLoad(url, context);
   112	}

   101	});

   103	test("detectWorkflowMcpLaunchConfig resolves the bundled server from GSD_BIN_PATH ancestry", () => {
   104	  const repoRoot = mkdtempSync(join(tmpdir(), "gsd-workflow-root-"));
   105	  const worktreeRoot = mkdtempSync(join(tmpdir(), "gsd-workflow-worktree-"));
   106	  const cliPath = join(repoRoot, "packages", "mcp-server", "dist", "cli.js");
   107	  const devCliPath = join(repoRoot, "scripts", "dev-cli.js");
   108	
   109	  mkdirSync(join(repoRoot, "packages", "mcp-server", "dist"), { recursive: true });
   110	  mkdirSync(join(repoRoot, "scripts"), { recursive: true });
   111	  writeFileSync(cliPath, "#!/usr/bin/env node\n", "utf-8");
   112	  writeFileSync(devCliPath, "#!/usr/bin/env node\n", "utf-8");
   113	
   114	  const launch = detectWorkflowMcpLaunchConfig(worktreeRoot, {
   115	    GSD_BIN_PATH: devCliPath,
   116	  });

   118	  assert.deepEqual(launch, {
   119	    name: "gsd-workflow",
   120	    command: process.execPath,

   122	    cwd: worktreeRoot,
   123	    env: launch?.env,
   124	  });
   125	  assert.equal(launch?.env?.GSD_CLI_PATH, devCliPath);
   126	  assert.equal(launch?.env?.GSD_PERSIST_WRITE_GATE_STATE, "1");
   127	  assert.equal(launch?.env?.GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT, worktreeRoot);
   128	  assert.match(launch?.env?.GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE ?? "", /workflow-tool-executors\.(js|ts)$/);
   129	  assert.match(launch?.env?.GSD_WORKFLOW_WRITE_GATE_MODULE ?? "", /write-gate\.(js|ts)$/);
   130	});

str_replace_editor create /testbed/packages/mcp-server/src/ask-user-questions.ts --file_text 'import { z } from "zod";

type TextContent = { type: "text"; text: string };

type ToolResult = { content: TextContent[]; isError?: true };

type ElicitResult = {
  action: "accept" | "decline" | "cancel";
  content?: Record<string, string | number | boolean | string[]>;
};

type ElicitCapableServer = {
  tool(
    name: string,
    description: string,
    params: Record<string, unknown>,
    handler: (args: Record<string, unknown>, extra?: unknown) => Promise<unknown>,
  ): unknown;
  server?: {
    elicitInput?: (params: Record<string, unknown>, options?: unknown) => Promise<ElicitResult>;
  };
};

const OTHER_OPTION_LABEL = "None of the above";
const NOTE_SUFFIX = "__note";

const optionSchema = z.object({
  label: z.string().describe("User-facing label (1-5 words)"),
  description: z.string().describe("One short sentence explaining impact/tradeoff if selected"),
});

const questionSchema = z.object({
  id: z.string().describe("Stable identifier for mapping answers (snake_case)"),
  header: z.string().describe("Short header label shown in the UI"),
  question: z.string().describe("Single-sentence prompt shown to the user"),
  options: z.array(optionSchema).describe("Concrete choices to present to the user"),
  allowMultiple: z.boolean().optional().describe("If true, the user can select multiple options"),
});

const askUserQuestionsParams = {
  questions: z.array(questionSchema).describe("Questions to show the user. Prefer 1 and do not exceed 3."),
};

const askUserQuestionsSchema = z.object(askUserQuestionsParams);

type AskUserQuestion = z.infer<typeof questionSchema>;

function jsonToolResult(data: unknown): ToolResult {
  return { content: [{ type: "text", text: JSON.stringify(data) }] };
}

function errorToolResult(message: string): ToolResult {
  return { isError: true, content: [{ type: "text", text: message }] };
}

function uniqueOptionLabels(question: AskUserQuestion): string[] {
  const labels = question.options.map((option) => option.label).filter((label) => label.trim().length > 0);
  if (!question.allowMultiple && !labels.includes(OTHER_OPTION_LABEL)) {
    labels.push(OTHER_OPTION_LABEL);
  }
  return [...new Set(labels)];
}

function buildElicitationMessage(questions: AskUserQuestion[]): string {
  const lines = ["GSD needs your input to continue."];
  for (const question of questions) {
    lines.push("", `${question.header}: ${question.question}`);
    for (const option of question.options) {
      lines.push(`- ${option.label}${option.description ? ` — ${option.description}` : ""}`);
    }
    if (!question.allowMultiple) {
      lines.push(`- ${OTHER_OPTION_LABEL} — Choose this if none of the listed options fit, then add context in the note field.`);
    }
  }
  return lines.join("\n");
}

function buildRequestedSchema(questions: AskUserQuestion[]): Record<string, unknown> {
  const properties: Record<string, unknown> = {};
  const required: string[] = [];

  for (const question of questions) {
    const labels = uniqueOptionLabels(question);
    required.push(question.id);
    if (question.allowMultiple) {
      properties[question.id] = {
        type: "array",
        title: question.header,
        description: question.question,
        items: { type: "string", enum: labels },
        default: [],
      };
    } else {
      properties[question.id] = {
        type: "string",
        title: question.header,
        description: question.question,
        enum: labels,
        default: labels[0],
      };
    }

    properties[`${question.id}${NOTE_SUFFIX}`] = {
      type: "string",
      title: `${question.header} note`,
      description: "Optional free-form context for this answer.",
    };
  }

  return {
    type: "object",
    properties,
    required,
  };
}

function formatAcceptedAnswers(
  questions: AskUserQuestion[],
  content: Record<string, string | number | boolean | string[]>,
): { answers: Record<string, { answers: string[] }> } {
  const answers: Record<string, { answers: string[] }> = {};

  for (const question of questions) {
    const rawAnswer = content[question.id];
    const answerList = Array.isArray(rawAnswer)
      ? rawAnswer.map(String)
      : rawAnswer === undefined || rawAnswer === null
        ? []
        : [String(rawAnswer)];

    const rawNote = content[`${question.id}${NOTE_SUFFIX}`];
    if (typeof rawNote === "string" && rawNote.trim().length > 0) {
      answerList.push(`user_note: ${rawNote.trim()}`);
    }

    answers[question.id] = { answers: answerList };
  }

  return { answers };
}

export function registerAskUserQuestionsTool(server: ElicitCapableServer): void {
  server.tool(
    "ask_user_questions",
    "Ask the user one to three structured questions using MCP form elicitation and return GSD-compatible answer JSON.",
    askUserQuestionsParams,
    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
      const parsed = askUserQuestionsSchema.parse(args);

      if (parsed.questions.length === 0 || parsed.questions.length > 3) {
        return errorToolResult("ask_user_questions: questions must contain 1-3 items");
      }
      for (const question of parsed.questions) {
        if (question.options.length === 0) {
          return errorToolResult(`ask_user_questions: question \"${question.id}\" must include at least one option`);
        }
      }

      const elicitInput = server.server?.elicitInput;
      if (typeof elicitInput !== "function") {
        return errorToolResult("ask_user_questions: MCP form elicitation is not available on this server");
      }

      let result: ElicitResult;
      try {
        result = await elicitInput.call(server.server, {
          mode: "form",
          message: buildElicitationMessage(parsed.questions),
          requestedSchema: buildRequestedSchema(parsed.questions),
        });
      } catch (err) {
        return errorToolResult(`ask_user_questions: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`);
      }

      if (result.action !== "accept" || !result.content) {
        return errorToolResult(`ask_user_questions: user ${result.action === "decline" ? "declined" : "cancelled"} the request`);
      }

      return jsonToolResult(formatAcceptedAnswers(parsed.questions, result.content));
    },
  );
}

     2	
     3	/**
     4	 * @gsd-build/mcp-server CLI — stdio transport entry point.
     5	 *
     6	 * Connects the MCP server to stdin/stdout for use by Claude Code,
     7	 * Cursor, and other MCP-compatible clients.
     8	 */
     9	
    10	import { SessionManager } from './session-manager.js';
    11	import { createMcpServer } from './server.js';
    12	
    13	const MCP_PKG = '@modelcontextprotocol/sdk';
    14	
    15	async function main(): Promise<void> {
    16	  const sessionManager = new SessionManager();
    17	
    18	  // Create the configured MCP server with all 12 tools (6 session + 6 read-only)
    19	  const { server } = await createMcpServer(sessionManager);
    20	
    21	  // Dynamic import for StdioServerTransport (same TS subpath workaround)
    22	  const { StdioServerTransport } = await import(`${MCP_PKG}/server/stdio.js`);
    23	  const transport = new StdioServerTransport();
    24	
    25	  // Cleanup handler — stop all sessions before exiting
    26	  let cleaningUp = false;
    27	  async function cleanup(): Promise<void> {
    28	    if (cleaningUp) return;
    29	    cleaningUp = true;
    30	    process.stderr.write('[gsd-mcp-server] Shutting down...\n');
    31	    try {
    32	      await sessionManager.cleanup();
    33	    } catch {
    34	      // swallow cleanup errors
    35	    }
    36	    try {
    37	      await server.close();
    38	    } catch {
    39	      // swallow close errors
    40	    }
    41	    process.exit(0);
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  process.on('SIGTERM', () => void cleanup());
    45	  process.on('SIGINT', () => void cleanup());
    46	
    47	  // Handle stdin end — MCP client disconnected
    48	  process.stdin.on('end', () => void cleanup());
    49	
    50	  // Connect and start serving
    51	  try {
    52	    await server.connect(transport);
    53	    process.stderr.write('[gsd-mcp-server] MCP server started on stdio\n');
    54	  } catch (err) {
    55	    process.stderr.write(
    56	      `[gsd-mcp-server] Fatal: failed to start — ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}\n`
    57	    );
    58	    await sessionManager.cleanup();
    59	    process.exit(1);
    60	  }
    61	}
    62	
    63	main().catch((err) => {
    64	  process.stderr.write(
    65	    `[gsd-mcp-server] Fatal: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}\n`
    66	  );
    67	  process.exit(1);
    68	});

    if (existsSync(candidate)) return candidate;

function parseNodeOptions(value: string | undefined): string[] {
  if (!value) return [];
  // NODE_OPTIONS used here is controlled by the local process/test harness.  A
  // whitespace split is sufficient for the flags we care about (--import and
  // --experimental-strip-types), and avoids pulling in shell parsing logic.
  return value.split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean);
}

function normalizeImportSpecifier(specifier: string): string {
  if (specifier.startsWith("file:")) return fileURLToPath(specifier);
  if (/^[a-z]{2,}:/i.test(specifier)) return specifier;
  return resolve(specifier);
}

function getActiveTsResolveHookArgs(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env): string[] | null {
  const argv = [...process.execArgv, ...parseNodeOptions(env.NODE_OPTIONS)];
  let hook: string | null = null;

  for (let i = 0; i < argv.length; i += 1) {
    const current = argv[i];
    const value = current === "--import" ? argv[i + 1] : current.startsWith("--import=") ? current.slice("--import=".length) : null;
    if (!value) continue;
    const normalized = normalizeImportSpecifier(value);
    if (normalized.endsWith("resolve-ts.mjs") && existsSync(normalized)) {
      hook = normalized;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (!hook) return null;
  return ["--import", hook, "--experimental-strip-types"];
}

const { registerAskUserQuestionsTool } = await import('./packages/mcp-server/dist/ask-user-questions.js');
let registered;
const fakeServer = {
  server: {
    async elicitInput(params) {
      if (params.mode !== 'form') throw new Error('expected form mode');
      return { action: 'accept', content: { direction: 'Ship now', direction__note: 'with guardrails', extras: ['Docs', 'Tests'] } };
    },
  },
  tool(name, description, params, handler) { registered = { name, description, params, handler }; },
};
registerAskUserQuestionsTool(fakeServer);
const result = await registered.handler({ questions: [
  { id: 'direction', header: 'Direction', question: 'What next?', options: [{ label: 'Ship now', description: 'Release' }, { label: 'Wait', description: 'Delay' }] },
  { id: 'extras', header: 'Extras', question: 'What else?', allowMultiple: true, options: [{ label: 'Docs', description: 'Docs' }, { label: 'Tests', description: 'Tests' }] },
] });
console.log(result.content[0].text);
const parsed = JSON.parse(result.content[0].text);
if (parsed.answers.direction.answers[0] !== 'Ship now') process.exit(1);
if (parsed.answers.direction.answers[1] !== 'user_note: with guardrails') process.exit(1);
if (parsed.answers.extras.answers.length !== 2) process.exit(1);
EOF
